She has a soft, playful smirk and is looking slightly off-camera. Her dark brown hair is wet and slicked back, suggesting she has just been swimming.
```
Clothing
She is wearing a classic {argument name="bikini color" default="black"} two-piece bikini. The top features a twist-front bandeau design with thin halter straps, while the bottoms have a delicate ruffled trim along the edges.
Setting & Atmosphere
The scene is set against a backdrop of a vast body of water, likely a lake, with dark green-grey ripples catching the light. The wooden dock beneath her is weathered and damp. The overall mood is relaxed and summery, captured in natural, slightly diffused daylight that highlights the moisture on her skin.
Composition & Style
The composition is a balanced medium shot with a relatively shallow depth of field, keeping the focus sharp on the woman while the water in the background is softly blurred. The color palette is naturalistic and muted, dominated by the deep tones of the water, the warm wood of the dock, and the stark black of her swimwear."
```

> 一个详细的提示，用于生成一张高定时装编辑肖像照：一位酷似安娜·德·阿玛斯 (Ana de Armas) 的女性，浸没在祖母绿色的天然水池中。重点在于湿发物理效果、玻璃肌效果、精致的化妆细节（水钻、闪粉），以及水体动态与焦散光反射的相互作用，旨在营造一种空灵、仙境般的氛围。

### 18. JSON 提示词：逼真的缎面迷你连衣裙镜面自拍

**Author**: [Mirabelle♡](https://x.com/Xmira_belle)  **Date**: 2026-02-05  **Language**: en

> 一个高度结构化的 JSON 提示词，用于 Gemini Nano Banana Pro，请求生成一张年轻女性（Sadie Sink 的相似者）在卧室里拍摄的逼真 4K/8K 镜面自拍照，她身穿紧身、反光的深勃艮第色缎面迷你连衣裙，背景是黑胶唱片和温暖的室内灯光。

```
{
  "prompt_generation": {
    "subject": {
      "type": "Young woman",
      "action": "Taking a mirror selfie",
      "pose": "Standing, slightly angled, one hip popped, right hand holding smartphone, left hand resting near thigh",
      "hair": "Long, brunette, loose waves, parted in the middle, falling over shoulders",
      "expression": "Soft, neutral pout, gaze directed at phone screen"
    },
    "outfit": {
      "garment": "Mini dress",
      "color": "Deep burgundy / Wine red",
      "fabric": "Satin or Silk",
      "texture": "High sheen, reflective, smooth",
      "style": "Bodycon, tight-fitting, cowl neckline, sleeveless, ruched detailing at the waist"
    },
    "accessories": {
      "jewelry": "Delicate thin gold chain necklace",
      "phone": "Modern smartphone (iPhone pro style)",
      "phone_case": "White case covered in black and white graphic collage or manga-panel style stickers"
    },
    "environment": {
      "setting": "Bedroom interior",
      "foreground": "Large full-length mirror with a thick, rustic brown wooden frame",
      "background_elements": [
        "Teal/turquoise curtains at the top",
        "White door with a gold handle on the right",
        "Four vinyl records mounted in a 2x2 grid on the right wall",
        "Partial view of vinyl records and artwork on the left wall",
        "White dresser or shelving unit on the left",
        "Beige carpeted floor"
      ]
    },
    "lighting": {
      "source": "Indoor artificial overhead lighting",
      "characteristics": "Warm tones, casting distinct shadows on the white walls to the right",
      "reflections": "High contrast reflections on the satin dress fabric"
    },
    "image_quality": {
      "resolution": "4K, 8K, Ultra HD",
      "fidelity": "Photorealistic, hyper-detailed",
      "focus": "Sharp focus on subject, realistic textures",
      "aesthetic": "Candid social media aesthetic, mirror selfie style, high-quality phone photography"
    }
  },
  "full_prompt_string": "A photorealistic 4k mirror selfie of a young woman with long wavy brunette hair, wearing a tight deep burgundy satin mini dress with a cowl neck. **Author**: [ANKIT PATEL 🇮🇳 | AI](https://x.com/Ankit_patel211)  **Date**: 2026-04-07  **Language**: en
```

> 一份详细的提示词，用于生成一张逼真的全身照，展示一位酷似 Madelyn Cline 的年轻女性在明亮的健身房内穿着淡紫色 Garfield T 恤进行深蹲。

Kodak Portra 160 film stock emulation, authentic analog grain, profound tactile realism, completely devoid of neon or digital illustration artifacts. High dynamic range with a distinct cinematic film curve, protecting highlights on the waxy corn. Pronounced analog film grain (Kodak Portra 160), emphasizing physical skin pores and plant cell structures. Zero artificial sharpening; relying entirely on the pristine optical clarity of the macro lens. Extremely subtle edge fringing in the deep out-of-focus areas to mimic vintage glass. Numerous 3D Spotify and Apple Music interface cards orbiting Drake at varying depths.
```
Material: Translucent frosted glass (glassmorphism) with soft rounded edges and subtle glowing borders.
 Movement: Some cards are in the extreme foreground, partially obscuring Drake, while others drift into the distance behind him.
Visual Accents: Dynamic motion blur on the edges of the cards to suggest a swirling, orbiting movement.
LIGHTING & COMPOSITION
Lighting: Natural tones with enhanced professional photo quality. The soft glow from the interface cards subtly illuminates Drake’s face.
Focus: Strong depth of field. The background and extreme foreground cards are artistically blurred, keeping the focus sharp on Drake and the closest player interfaces.
Composition: A cinematic wide or medium shot that emphasizes the scale of the floating AR elements.
AESTHETIC
High-end editorial music photography, futuristic AR concept, clean and airy vibe. 8k resolution, sophisticated lighting, and realistic textures on the glass cards.
```

> 一个高度结构化的 JSON 提示，用于生成安娜·德·阿玛斯（Ana de Armas）在夜晚的超写实电影中景镜头。场景设定在俯瞰城市天际线的玻璃阳台上，金色反光主导着光线。提示详细说明了她的外貌（金色头发、白皙皮肤、合身米色连衣裙，带有金色花卉图案），并对脸部特征和胸部尺寸施加了严格的解剖学约束，以匹配参考图像。

![安娜·德·阿玛斯 (Ana de Armas) 的超现实电影级夜景镜头](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769322307594_67ab6k_G_azkQfXoAAgZkc.jpg)
![安娜·德·阿玛斯 (Ana de Armas) 的超现实电影级夜景镜头](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769322307573_2ropy4_G_azkQeXcAALE9y.jpg)
![安娜·德·阿玛斯 (Ana de Armas) 的超现实电影级夜景镜头](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769322307699_gnnyng_G_azkQeXQAAElEv.jpg)
